<DLGNAME>LayerPropertiesManagerDLG</DLGNAME>
<STEPS>
Launch AutoCAD Plant 3D product.
New one Plant 3D drawing file.
Click Home tab->Route Pipe, then draw one pipe in the drawing area.
Click Home tab->Ortho Views panel->Create Ortho View button.
Click "Create New..." button in invoked "Select Orthographic Drawing" dialog.
Input the file name then click OK in New DWG dialog.
In invoked Ortho Editor tab, select "Solid Line Insulation" dropdown list item from Output Appearance panel.
Click OK in Ortho Editor tab
Put the created ortho view into drawing area by click left mouse.
Click Ortho View tab->Layer Properties button.		
</STEPS>

<DLGNAME>PlantUndoCheckOutDLG</DLGNAME>
<STEPS>
Launch Autodesk Plant3D product.
Sign in to Autodesk account.
Type at the Command Line: "_NEWPROJECT".
Enter a project name then click next to finish .
Type at the Command Line: "_PLANTPROJECTCOLLABORATION"
Click Get Start in Plant Project Collaboration.
Select PLANT3D in list(if there is no PLANT3D ,should create a PLANT3D Folder in BIM360) ,click Upload Project.this (step may take lone time)
After Complate ,Select“Open Collaboration Project” in PROJECT MANAGER popuplist.
In Open Collaboration Project dialog select the project name you upload in step 
Click Open Project button.
Right click" Plant 3D Drawing "In PROJECT MANAGER,select "New Drawing..' new a drawing.
Type at the command Line:: "_PlantCheckIn".
Click OK .
Right click the drawing you create in step 11,select "Check Out..".
Right click the drawing you create in step 11,select "Open".
Type at the command Line:: "_PLANTPIPEADD".
Type at the command Line:: "20".
Type at the command Line:: "100".
Type at the command Line:"<Enter>"
Type at the command Line:"_PLANTUNDOCHECKOUT"
</STEPS>

<DLGNAME>FileSetToReadOnlyDLG</DLGNAME>
<STEPS>
Launch AutoCAD Plant3D 201x.
Create a new project.
Right click the ‘Plant3D Drawings’, select ‘New Drawing…’ and create a new drawing named ‘ABC.DWG’.
Close the drawing.
Right click the ‘ABC.dwg’ drawing in the ‘PROJECT MANAGER’ palette and select ‘Remove Drawing’.
Click ‘OK’ in the ‘Remove Drawings From Project’ dialog.
In Windows explorer Under project folder in '...\PLANT3D DWG' mark the 'ABC.DWG' file as read-only
Back in AutoCAD PLANT3D right click the ‘Plant3D Drawings’, select ‘New Drawing…’ and try to create a new drawing named again ‘ABC.DWG’.
Localized ‘AutoCAD P&ID - This FIle is set...' dialog is invoked.
</STEPS>

<DLGNAME>DrawingAlreadyExistsDLG</DLGNAME>
<STEPS>
Launch Autodesk Plant3D product.
Create a new project.
Right click the ‘Plant3d Drawings’, select ‘New Drawing…’ and create a new drawing named ‘ABC.DWG’.
Close the drawing.
Now open the 'ABC.DWG' in a new instance of the Autodesk Plant3D. or in another application.
Back in the Autodesk Plant3D. Right click the ‘ABC.dwg’ drawing in the ‘PROJECT MANAGER’ palette and select ‘Remove Drawing’.
Type 'ABC.DWG' in the 'New.DWG' dialog and click 'OK" button.
Localized ‘Drawing Already Exists' dialog is invoked.
</STEPS>

Launch AutoCAD Plant 3D Spec Editor 2013

Enter same name as in previous steps (e.g. Test) in the ‘Block Compatible Standard:’ text box, select ‘Imperial’ from ‘Units’ dropdown and enter bolt information to ‘Bolt lengths to include’ table

<DLGNAME>PandIDNoneBlockInsideThisDWGDLG</DLGNAME>
<STEPS>
Launch AutoCAD Plant3D Catalog Builder - e.g. from c:\Program Files\Autodesk\AutoCAD 2026\PLANT3D\AutoCADPLANT3DCatalogBuilder.exe
Select a template under 'Recent Templates' (or create a new one) to invoke main 'Catalog Builder' application.

Select 'All/Cross' class name.
Click 'New' ribbon in the 'Part Familes' ribbon panel
Click 'Custom - AutoCAD DWG Block based graphics' radio button
Click the '...' ellipses next the 'Select DWG file containing blocks:'
Select a DWG file where were blocks converted using ‘PLANTPARTCONVERT’ command (can't provide a sample file via testkit as the file have to be a part of a project. 
Note: To prepare such DWG simply send PLANTPARTCONVERT command in Plant 3D application, select a block and define the connection parts, then save and close the drawing in Plant 3D - see steps below: 
- Send ‘SPHERE’ command and create a pipe 
- Select the pipe and send ‘_BLOCK’ command. 
- Enter a block name and click ‘OK’ to close ‘Block Definition’ dialog. 
- Send ‘_PLANTPARTCONVERT’ command, select the create block to convert, send ‘Add’ option, specify a point on the block (port location), specify a direction of the new port (port direction), send ‘Accept option and then ‘Exit’ option. 
</STEPS>

<DLGNAME>PandIDStyleAlreadyExistsInDrawingErrorDLG</DLGNAME>
<STEPS>
Launch AutoCAD Plant 3D 2012
Create a new project.
Send '_PROJECTSETUP' command.
Navigate to the 'P&ID Class Definitions' section (e.g. expand 'P&ID DWG Settings\P&ID Class Definition\Engineering Items\...'.
Click 'Add Symbols...' button
Click '...' button in 'Select Drawings:' section to invoke 'Select Block Drawing' dialog.
Select and open a DWG file with symbols (e.g. navigate 'to C:\Program Files\Autodesk\AutoCAD Plant 3D 2012\SymbolLibrary').
Select a block and click 'Add >>' to add blocks to 'Selected Blocks' list.
Click 'Next >>' to invoke 'Add Symbols - Edit Symbol Settings' dialog.
Click the '...' button next 'P&ID Class Definitions:' section, select a class, click 'OK' to see the new class is selected under 'P&ID Class Definitions:' text box.
Type ‘TEST’ in the ‘Symbol Name’ for the block. (Note: or type a block name of already existing block and then ignore steps 13-20)
Click ‘Finish’.
Click 'Add Symbols...' button
Click '...' button in 'Select Drawings:' section to invoke 'Select Block Drawing' dialog.
Select and open a DWG file with symbols (e.g. navigate 'to C:\Program Files\Autodesk\AutoCAD Plant 3D 2012\SymbolLibrary').
Select a block and click 'Add >>' to add blocks to 'Selected Blocks' list.
Click 'Next >>' to invoke 'Add Symbols - Edit Symbol Settings' dialog.
Click the '...' button next 'P&ID Class Definitions:' section, select a class, click 'OK' to see the new class is selected under 'P&ID Class Definitions:' text box.
Type identical name of already existing block – e.g. ‘TEST’ in the ‘Symbol Name’ for the block.
Click ‘Finish’.
</STEPS>

<DLGNAME>PandIDFileExistsDLG</DLGNAME>
<STEPS>
Launch AutoCAD Plant 3D 20
Create a new project.
Right click the ‘P&ID Drawings’, select ‘New Drawing…’ and create a new drawing named ‘ABC.DWG’.
Close the drawing.
Right click the ‘ABC.dwg’ drawing in the ‘PROJECT MANAGER’ palette and select ‘Remove Drawing’.
Click ‘OK’ in the ‘Remove Drawingfs From Project’ dialog.
Right click the ‘P&ID Drawings’, select ‘New Drawing…’ and try to create a new drawing named again ‘ABC.DWG’.
Localized ‘File Exists’ dialog is invoked.
</STEPS>
<DLGNAME>PandIDNetworkPathNotFoundDLG</DLGNAME>
<STEPS>
Launch AutoCAD Plant 3D 20
Open the project 'NetworkPath' from the TestKit (NetworkPath.7z).
The ‘AutoCAD Plant 3D Migration’ wizard appears. 
Go through the migration wizard by clicking ‘Next ‘, unmark the ‘Backup these files before migration (recommended)’ check box and click ‘Next, click ‘Finish’ once the project migration is completed.
After a while localized ‘Network Path Not Found’ dialog appears.
Click the ‘Show details’ icon to expand the dialog.
</STEPS>
<DLGNAME>PandIDAutoCADP3DFileOpenForEditingDLG</DLGNAME>
<STEPS>
Launch AutoCAD Plant 3D 20
Create a new project.
Right click the ‘P&ID Drawings’, select ‘New Drawing…’ and create a new drawing named ‘ABC.DWG’.
Close the drawing.
Right click the ‘ABC.dwg’ drawing in the ‘PROJECT MANAGER’ palette and select ‘Remove Drawing’.
Click ‘OK’ in the ‘Remove Drawings From Project’ dialog.
Now open the 'ABC.DWG' in a new instance of the AutoCAD PLANT 3D or in another application.
Back in the AutoCAD Plant 3D Right click the ‘ABC.dwg’ drawing in the ‘PROJECT MANAGER’ palette and select ‘Remove Drawing’.
Type 'ABC.DWG' in the 'New.DWG' dialog and click 'OK" button.
Click 'Overwrite the existing drawing with this one' link.
Localized ‘AutoCAD Plant 3D - This File is open for editing in another session or by another user' dialog is invoked.
</STEPS>

<DLGNAME>PandIDDrawingAlreadyExistsDLG</DLGNAME>
<STEPS>
Launch AutoCAD Plant 3D 20
Create a new project.
Right click the ‘P&ID Drawings’, select ‘New Drawing…’ and create a new drawing named ‘ABC.DWG’.
Close the drawing.
Right click the ‘ABC.dwg’ drawing in the ‘PROJECT MANAGER’ palette and select ‘Remove Drawing’.
Click ‘OK’ in the ‘Remove Drawings From Project’ dialog.
Now open the 'ABC.DWG' in a new instance of the AutoCAD PLANT 3D or in another application.
Back in the AutoCAD Plant 3D Right click the ‘ABC.dwg’ drawing in the ‘PROJECT MANAGER’ palette and select ‘Remove Drawing’.
Type 'ABC.DWG' in the 'New.DWG' dialog and click 'OK" button.
Localized ‘Drawing Already Exists' dialog is invoked.
</STEPS>

Click the 'Edit...' button
Select one report/drawing

Click the 'Details' button

Create new project. - Project1
Create a new drawing 'Drawing1.DWG' under 'Plant 3D Drawings' node
Close all drawings.
Modify the 'Drawing1.DWG' using another project 
or take a drawing from another project, rename it to 'Drawing1.DWG' 
and replace the original drawing with the updated drawing under '...\Project1\Plant3D Models\' folder.
Mark the drawing as Read-only using Windows Explorer.
Double click the Drawing1 under 'Plant 3D Drawings' in the Plant3D.
</STEPS>

Click the 'Run Designer' link in the menu.
Click the 'Layout' icon under 'Main' group.
Select 'Load Data from XML' tab.
Click the 'Load XML File...' button.
Select and open a XML file."
</STEPS>

<DLGNAME>PandIDFileSetToReadOnlyDLG</DLGNAME>
<STEPS>
Launch AutoCAD Plant 3D 20
Create a new project.
Right click the ‘P&ID Drawings’, select ‘New Drawing…’ and create a new drawing named ‘ABC.DWG’.
Close the drawing.
Right click the ‘ABC.dwg’ drawing in the ‘PROJECT MANAGER’ palette and select ‘Remove Drawing’.
Click ‘OK’ in the ‘Remove Drawingfs From Project’ dialog.
In Windows explorer Under project folder in '...\PID DWG' mark the 'ABC.DWG' file as read-only
Back in AUtoCAD Plant 3D right click the ‘P&ID Drawings’, select ‘New Drawing…’ and try to create a new drawing named again ‘ABC.DWG’.
Localized ‘AutoCAD Plant 3D - This FIle is set...' dialog is invoked.
</STEPS>
<DLGNAME>PandIDReadOnlyDrawingErrorDLG</DLGNAME>
<STEPS>
Launch AutoCAD Plant 3D product.
Create new project. - Project1
Create a new drawing 'drawing1.dwg' under 'P&ID  Drawings' node.
Close the drawing.
Open the drawing  'drawing1.dwg' outside the 'project 1' (another application or another instance of P&ID)
Right click the 'drawing1' under Project1 and select 'Rename Drawing…'
Type a new name and click 'OK' - An alert 'File is Read Only' should be invoked. Click on 'Ok'

An alert dialog 'Read-only DWG Error' is invoked.

<DLGNAME>PandIDStyleAlreadyExistsInDrawingErrorDLG</DLGNAME>
<STEPS>
Launch AutoCAD Plant 3D product.
Create a new project.
Send '_PROJECTSETUP' command.
Navigate to the 'P&ID Class Definitions' section (e.g. expand 'P&ID DWG Settings\P&ID Class Definition\Engineering Items\...'.
Click 'Add Symbols...' button
Click '...' button in 'Select Drawings:' section to invoke 'Select Block Drawing' dialog.
Select and open a DWG file with symbols (e.g. navigate 'to C:\Program Files\Autodesk\AutoCAD P and ID 2012\SymbolLibrary').
Select a block and click 'Add >>' to add blocks to 'Selected Blocks' list.
Click 'Next >>' to invoke 'Add Symbols - Edit Symbol Settings' dialog.
Click the '...' button next 'P&ID Class Definitions:' section, select a class, click 'OK' to see the new class is selected under 'P&ID Class Definitions:' text box.
Type ‘TEST’ in the ‘Symbol Name’ for the block. (Note: or type a block name of already existing block and then ignore steps 13-20)
Click ‘Finish’.
Click 'Add Symbols...' button
Click '...' button in 'Select Drawings:' section to invoke 'Select Block Drawing' dialog.
Select and open a DWG file with symbols (e.g. navigate 'to C:\Program Files\Autodesk\AutoCAD P and ID 2012\SymbolLibrary').
Select a block and click 'Add >>' to add blocks to 'Selected Blocks' list.
Click 'Next >>' to invoke 'Add Symbols - Edit Symbol Settings' dialog.
Click the '...' button next 'P&ID Class Definitions:' section, select a class, click 'OK' to see the new class is selected under 'P&ID Class Definitions:' text box.
Type identical name of already existing block – e.g. ‘TEST’ in the ‘Symbol Name’ for the block.
Click ‘Finish’.
</STEPS>

Click 'Next' to invoke 'Add Symbols - Edit Symbol Settings' dialog.
Click the 'Next' button without defining class and symbol names to invoke 'Class Definition or Symbol Name Required' error dialog
</STEPS>

<STEPS>

Create new project. - Project1

Close all drawings.

<DLGNAME>PandIDFileExistsDLG</DLGNAME>
<STEPS>
Launch AutoCAD Plant 3D product..
Create a new project.
Right click the ‘P&ID Drawings’, select ‘New Drawing…’ and create a new drawing named ‘ABC.DWG’.
Close the drawing.
Right click the ‘ABC.dwg’ drawing in the ‘PROJECT MANAGER’ palette and select ‘Remove Drawing’.
Click ‘OK’ in the ‘Remove Drawingfs From Project’ dialog.
Right click the ‘P&ID Drawings’, select ‘New Drawing…’ and try to create a new drawing named again ‘ABC.DWG’.
Localized ‘File Exists’ dialog is invoked.
</STEPS>
<DLGNAME>PandIDNetworkPathNotFoundDLG</DLGNAME>
<STEPS>
Launch AutoCAD Plant 3D product..
Open the project 'NetworkPath' from the TestKit (NetworkPath.7z).
The ‘AutoCAD P and ID Migration’ wizard appears. 
Go through the migration wizard by clicking ‘Next ‘, unmark the ‘Backup these files before migration (recommended)’ check box and click ‘Next, click ‘Finish’ once the project migration is completed.
After a while localized ‘Network Path Not Found’ dialog appears.
Click the ‘Show details’ icon to expand the dialog.
</STEPS>
<DLGNAME>PandIDAutoCADPIDFileOpenForEditingDLG</DLGNAME>
<STEPS>
Launch AutoCAD Plant 3D product..
Create a new project.
Right click the ‘P&ID Drawings’, select ‘New Drawing…’ and create a new drawing named ‘ABC.DWG’.
Close the drawing.
Now open the 'ABC.DWG' in a new instance of the AutoCAD P and ID or in another application.
Back in the AutoCAD P and ID Right click the ‘ABC.dwg’ drawing in the ‘PROJECT MANAGER’ palette and select ‘Remove Drawing’.
Type 'ABC.DWG' in the 'New.DWG' dialog and click 'OK" button.
Click 'Overwrite the existing drawing with this one' link.
Localized ‘AutoCAD P and ID - This File is open for editing in another session or by another user' dialog is invoked.
</STEPS>

<DLGNAME>PandIDStyleAlreadyExistsInDrawingErrorDLG</DLGNAME>
<STEPS>
Launch AutoCAD Plant 3D product.
Create a new project.
Send '_PROJECTSETUP' command.
Navigate to the 'P&ID Class Definitions' section (e.g. expand 'P&ID DWG Settings\P&ID Class Definition\Engineering Items\...'.
Click 'Add Symbols...' button
Click '...' button in 'Select Drawings:' section to invoke 'Select Block Drawing' dialog.
Select and open a DWG file with symbols (e.g. navigate 'to C:\Program Files\Autodesk\AutoCAD P and ID 2012\SymbolLibrary').
Select a block and click 'Add >>' to add blocks to 'Selected Blocks' list.
Click 'Next >>' to invoke 'Add Symbols - Edit Symbol Settings' dialog.
Click the '...' button next 'P&ID Class Definitions:' section, select a class, click 'OK' to see the new class is selected under 'P&ID Class Definitions:' text box.
Type ‘TEST’ in the ‘Symbol Name’ for the block. (Note: or type a block name of already existing block and then ignore steps 13-20)
Click ‘Finish’.
Click 'Add Symbols...' button
Click '...' button in 'Select Drawings:' section to invoke 'Select Block Drawing' dialog.
Select and open a DWG file with symbols (e.g. navigate 'to C:\Program Files\Autodesk\AutoCAD P and ID 2012\SymbolLibrary').
Select a block and click 'Add >>' to add blocks to 'Selected Blocks' list.
Click 'Next >>' to invoke 'Add Symbols - Edit Symbol Settings' dialog.
Click the '...' button next 'P&ID Class Definitions:' section, select a class, click 'OK' to see the new class is selected under 'P&ID Class Definitions:' text box.
Type identical name of already existing block – e.g. ‘TEST’ in the ‘Symbol Name’ for the block.
Click ‘Finish’.
</STEPS>

<DLGNAME>PandIDFileExistsDLG</DLGNAME>
<STEPS>
Launch AutoCAD Plant 3D product..
Create a new project.
Right click the ‘P&ID Drawings’, select ‘New Drawing…’ and create a new drawing named ‘ABC.DWG’.
Close the drawing.
Right click the ‘ABC.dwg’ drawing in the ‘PROJECT MANAGER’ palette and select ‘Remove Drawing’.
Click ‘OK’ in the ‘Remove Drawingfs From Project’ dialog.
Right click the ‘P&ID Drawings’, select ‘New Drawing…’ and try to create a new drawing named again ‘ABC.DWG’.
Localized ‘File Exists’ dialog is invoked.
</STEPS>
<DLGNAME>PandIDNetworkPathNotFoundDLG</DLGNAME>
<STEPS>
Launch AutoCAD Plant 3D product..
Open the project 'NetworkPath' from the TestKit (NetworkPath.7z).
The ‘AutoCAD P and ID Migration’ wizard appears. 
Go through the migration wizard by clicking ‘Next ‘, unmark the ‘Backup these files before migration (recommended)’ check box and click ‘Next, click ‘Finish’ once the project migration is completed.
After a while localized ‘Network Path Not Found’ dialog appears.
Click the ‘Show details’ icon to expand the dialog.
</STEPS>
<DLGNAME>PandIDAutoCADPIDFileOpenForEditingDLG</DLGNAME>
<STEPS>
Launch AutoCAD Plant 3D product..
Create a new project.
Right click the ‘P&ID Drawings’, select ‘New Drawing…’ and create a new drawing named ‘ABC.DWG’.
Close the drawing.
Now open the 'ABC.DWG' in a new instance of the AutoCAD P and ID or in another application.
Back in the AutoCAD P and ID Right click the ‘ABC.dwg’ drawing in the ‘PROJECT MANAGER’ palette and select ‘Remove Drawing’.
Type 'ABC.DWG' in the 'New.DWG' dialog and click 'OK" button.
Click 'Overwrite the existing drawing with this one' link.
Localized ‘AutoCAD P and ID - This File is open for editing in another session or by another user' dialog is invoked.
</STEPS>

<STEPS>

<DLGNAME>PandIDDuplicateNameMSG</DLGNAME>
<STEPS>
Launch Autodesk Plant3D product.
Type at the Command Line: "_PROJECTSETUP".
In "Project Setup" dialog box expand "Project Setting" tree and in that expand the "General".
In "General" click on "End Connection". It invokes "ProjectSetupEndConnection" dialog box.
In "End Connection" dialog box click to "Add Block..." button. It invokes "New End Connection" dialog box.
In "New End Connection" dialog box enter the already existing end connection name say (Flanged) and click the "Browse..." button and open the file ProjSymbolstyle from Test Kit.
After that following dialog box "Select Block" appears.
Select any block (say SINGLE LINE NOZZLE) and click to "OK".
It invokes the dialog "SelectBlockError".
Click "Yes" button.
Now the "New End Connection" dialog box has both end connection name and block definition.
Click "OK" button of "New End Connection" dialog box.
It invokes the "Duplicate Name" dialog box.
</STEPS>

<DLGNAME>PandIDSegmentDataDiffersTaskDLG</DLGNAME>
<STEPS>
Open any Sample Project.
Add two drawings under P&ID Drawings.
In the drawing area add a vertical sline.
Insert a vertical inline pump midway between the sline.
Select the upper sline, right click on it and select Assign Tag.
In the Assign tag dialog, set the Pipe Line Group Line Number as '1' and click on Assign button.
Similarly assign the tag '2' to the lower part of  the sline.
Now click on the vertical inline pump to select it.  
Press DEL key to delete it.
The Segment Data Differs task dialog is displayed.
</STEPS>

<DLGNAME>CheckInSettingsDLG</DLGNAME>
<STEPS>
Install Plant 3D.
Install VP + VP server.
Launch Sql Server Configration Manager from start menu, expand SQL Server Network Configuration->Protocls for AUTODESKVAULT, RMB the Named Pipes item and Enable it, RMB TCP/IP item and select Properties item, select IP Addresses tab, select Yes for Enabled item under IP4 region, set TCP Dynamic Ports as "1433". OK the TCP/IP Properties dialog.
Select "SQL Server Servies" item from SQL Server Configuration Manager dialog, RMB on SQL Server (AUTODESKVAULT) item and click on Restart item.
Launch VP Server and login with default settings, new vault name with "Vault". Launch VP and login to VP server.
Launch Plant 3D, In Project Manager window, click Current Project dropdown list then select "New Project..." item.
Enter project name, check on "Create this project in vault" checkbox, login with default settings. Click Next to go to "Project Setup Wizard (Page 5 of 6) dialog.
Enter "127.0.0.1\AUTODESKVAULT,1433"（"127.0.0.1\MSSSQLSERVER,1433" as SQL Servername, click on Test Connection button. The Connection Succeeded dialog will pop up. OK it.
Click Next then click Finish button to finish the vault project creation.
Open the created Vault Project.
New a Plant 3D drawing file.
Select the created Plant 3D drawing file
Right click and select "Check In"
Click "Settings" button.
</STEPS>

Enter "127.0.0.1\AUTODESKVAULT,1433"（"127.0.0.1\MSSSQLSERVER,1433" as SQL Servername, click on Test Connection button. The Connection Succeeded dialog will pop up. OK it.
Click Next then click Finish button to finish the vault project creation.
Open the created Vault Project.
New a Plant 3D drawing file.
Right click on the created Plant 3D drawing file select Check in item.

<STEPS>
Install Plant 3D.
Install VP + VP server.
Launch Sql Server Configration Manager from start menu, expand SQL Server Network Configuration->Protocls for AUTODESKVAULT, RMB the Named Pipes item and Enable it, RMB TCP/IP item and select Properties item, select IP Addresses tab, select Yes for Enabled item under IP4 region, set TCP Dynamic Ports as "1433". OK the TCP/IP Properties dialog.
Select "SQL Server Servies" item from SQL Server Configuration Manager dialog, RMB on SQL Server (AUTODESKVAULT) item and click on Restart item.
Launch VP Server and login with default settings, new vault name with "Vault". Launch VP and login to VP server.
Launch Plant 3D, In Project Manager window, click Current Project dropdown list then select "New Project..." item.
Enter project name, check on "Create this project in vault" checkbox, login with default settings. Click Next to go to "Project Setup Wizard (Page 5 of 6) dialog.

<DLGNAME>ImportDataDLG</DLGNAME>
<STEPS>
Open one drawing file eg. "1-A1-1002.dwg in sample project->P&ID drawings in Plant 3D.
Click Home tab-> Project panel-> Data Manager button.
Select P&ID Project Data item in top left dropdown list.
Select Engineering->Nozzles->Flanged Nozzle item, click Export button in Data Manager dialog.
Input name for exported excel file and save. (Install Excell first)
Open the exported excel file, in Flanged Nozzle sheet, modify/update one column eg. Manufacturer. as below: Note: please use localization characters for testing. then save the file.
Switch back to Data Manager dialog, click Import button. Select the modified excel file and OK.
</STEPS>
<DLGNAME>Plant3DExcelImportDLG</DLGNAME>
<STEPS>
Open one drawing file eg. "1-A1-1002.dwg in sample project->P&ID drawings in Plant 3D.
Click Home tab-> Project panel-> Data Manager button.
Select P&ID Project Data item in top left dropdown list.
Select Engineering->Nozzles->Flanged Nozzle item, click Export button in Data Manager dialog.
Input name for exported excel file and save. (Install Excell first)
Open the exported excel file, in Flanged Nozzle sheet, modify/update one column eg. Manufacturer. as below: Note: please use localization characters for testing. then save the file.
Switch back to Data Manager dialog, click Import button. Select the modified excel file and OK.
Check the modified content in excel will be updated in Data Manager,
Click Accept All button in Data Manager, the Plant 3D - Excel Import dialog will be pop up. Check the UI display well, consistent with ENU. Check strings are localized correctly.
</STEPS>

<STEPS>

Select an orthographic view(pink line in drawing area), the menu display, click on "byLineNumber" menu item. (also try click on "byLineNumber" button in bottom command).

Launch Autodesk Plant3D product.
Create a new Imperial or Metric Project
Create a new drawing
Type at the Command Line: PROJECTSETUP to open Project setup dialog.
Go to Ortho DWG Settings->Tile Block and Display.
Click “Setup Title Block…”
Type at the Command Line: PLANTORTHOTEMPLATETABLESETUP.
CLick Settings tab.
Select  Piping BOM in the list.
Click Add button under Sort rows by.
</STEPS>

<DLGNAME>SynchronizeProjectToServerDLG</DLGNAME>
<STEPS>
Install Vault VP and VP server.
Launch Autodesk Plant3D product.
Send command :"_newproject"
Enter a project name, check on "Create this project in vault" checkbox, login with default settings. Click Next to go to "Project Setup Wizard (Page 5 of 6) dialog.
Enter "127.0.0.1\AUTODESKVAULT,1433" as SQL Servername, click on Test Connection button. The Connection Succeeded dialog will pop up. OK it.
Click Next then click Finish button to finish the vault project creation.
In PROJECTMANAGER dialog select the created Vault project under Current Project.
Create a Plant3D drawing under the VaultProject.
Type at the Command Line:"_PLANTPIPEADD"
Type at the Command Line:"20"
Type at the Command Line:"100"
Type at the Command Line:"<Enter>"
Type at the Command Line:"<Enter>"
Type at the Command Line:"<Enter>"
Create a new  Plant3D drawing under the VaultProject.
Type at the Command Line:"_PLANTPIPEADD"
Type at the Command Line:"20"
Type at the Command Line:"100"
Type at the Command Line:"<Enter>"
Type at the Command Line:"_PLANTSYNCHRONIZETOVAULT"
</STEPS>
<DLGNAME>SelectImageFileDLG</DLGNAME>
<STEPS>
Launch 'Report Creator for AutoCAD Plant 3D from Star menu .
Select a project in 'Project' dropdown
Select an item (except the 'New...') from 'Report Configuration' dropdown 
Select 'Edit...' button
Click the 'Edit report layout…' button
Click CTRL+N to create a New Report (OR from ribbon 'Report Designer ribbon tab->Report panel->New Report')
Click 'Chart' in the 'Tool Box', place it in the working area and  - a Chart Wizard appears.
Select 'Chart' .
Go to Properties tab
Click the ellipses '...' button next the 'Background Image' text box."
</STEPS>

Select"P&ID DWG Settings\Pipe Specs in P&ID\Pipe Spec Object Mapping"in Project Setup dialog.
Click second button Valves under P&ID Objects.
</STEPS>

<DLGNAME>ReviseDLG</DLGNAME>
<STEPS>
Install Plant 3D.
Install VP + VP server.
Launch Sql Server Configration Manager from start menu, expand SQL Server Network Configuration->Protocls for AUTODESKVAULT, RMB the Named Pipes item and Enable it, RMB TCP/IP item and select Properties item, select IP Addresses tab, select Yes for Enabled item under IP4 region, set TCP Dynamic Ports as "1433". OK the TCP/IP Properties dialog.
Select "SQL Server Servies" item from SQL Server Configuration Manager dialog, RMB on SQL Server (AUTODESKVAULT) item and click on Restart item.
Launch VP Server and login with default settings, new vault name with "Vault". Launch VP and login to VP server.
Launch Plant 3D, In Project Manager window, click Current Project dropdown list then select "New Project..." item.
Enter project name, check on "Create this project in vault" checkbox, login with default settings. Click Next to go to "Project Setup Wizard (Page 5 of 6) dialog.
Enter "127.0.0.1\AUTODESKVAULT,1433"（"127.0.0.1\MSSSQLSERVER,1433" as SQL Servername, click on Test Connection button. The Connection Succeeded dialog will pop up. OK it.
Click Next then click Finish button to finish the vault project creation.
Open the created Vault Project.
New a Plant 3D drawing file.
Select the created Plant 3D drawing file.
Right click and select "Check In", and Click "OK"
Select the checked-in Plant 3D drawing file
Right click and select "New Revise"
</STEPS>
<DLGNAME>DataSourceWizardDLG_SelectADataConnectionType</DLGNAME>
<STEPS>
Launch 'Report Creator for AutoCAD Plant 3D from Star menu .
Select a project in 'Project' dropdown
Select an item (except the 'New...') from 'Report Configuration' dropdown 
Select 'Edit...' button
Click the 'Edit report layout…' button
Click Add Data Source in ribbon Home tab
Select "No, I'd *",Click Next button.
</STEPS>
